     2→
     3→### 101
     4→All players must always abide by all the rules then in effect, in the form in which they are then in effect. The rules in the Initial Set are in effect whenever a game begins. The Initial Set consists of Rules 101-116 (immutable) and 201-215 (mutable).

   116→Voting on rule-changes uses a commit-reveal process. During the commit phase, each player submits a hash commitment of their vote using the `commit` tool. During the reveal phase, each player reveals their vote and nonce. The Clerk verifies each reveal against the commitment using the `verify` tool. A vote is invalid if the reveal does not match the commitment.
